        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2198047520" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4221305891680089783">I don’t have a very good relationship with John Green books, they are CLEARLY hit or miss for me (hit: TFIOS) (miss: Abundance of Katherines, Paper Towns, Let it Snow, Will Grayson x2) YOU CAN CLEARLY SEE MY DILEMMA IN PICKING UP THIS BOOK<br/><br/>But I was pleasantly surprised <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512144050i/24577930._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>So Turtles all the way down did have the john green elements i.e. <br/>-	Mental health rep<br/>-	Tragic characters with tragic backstories<br/>-	16 year old philosophers (it wasn’t so bad in this book)<br/>-	Hilarious best friends <br/>-	The ending that </span>
  <span id="freeText4221305891680089783" style="display:none">I don’t have a very good relationship with John Green books, they are CLEARLY hit or miss for me (hit: TFIOS) (miss: Abundance of Katherines, Paper Towns, Let it Snow, Will Grayson x2) YOU CAN CLEARLY SEE MY DILEMMA IN PICKING UP THIS BOOK<br><br>But I was pleasantly surprised <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512144050i/24577930._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>So Turtles all the way down did have the john green elements i.e. <br>-	Mental health rep<br>-	Tragic characters with tragic backstories<br>-	16 year old philosophers (it wasn’t so bad in this book)<br>-	Hilarious best friends <br>-	The ending that leaves you VERY unsatisfied <br><br>But this book was also unique in its own way in that<br>-	The characters felt more like themselves than fictional impersonators of mr. green<br>-	I thought the OCD was done FANTASTICALLY <br>-	The spiraling of thoughts and emotions and drag that is mental illness was incredible and maybe a little TOO real (but that’s not a negative in my book) <br>-	The best friend was 10/10 I loved her<br>-	SHE WRITES FANFICTION AND SHES THE FUNNIEST THING SINCE IDEK WHAT<br>-	The romance was kinda….quick…idk…it was alright, didn’t do anything great for me<br>-	The writing is VERY easy and I was able to read it in less than a day, so that’s a plus<br><br>The thing with john green books is that the endings are done in this cloaked dramatic flair where I feel like he’s either trying to SHOCK the reader or give them an ending that is so realistic is resonates with them, and that’s cool and all but I just find it to be so … emptying<br><br>Idk how to describe it but I could LOVE the entirety of all his books but the ending is given and then I go to legally change my name to disappointed bc that’s how I feel<br><br>There’s just always so much build up to something that’s just so simple and im like, I understand this isn’t supposed to be some great reveal, we aren’t reading epic fantasy here, but maybe a little something with a twist, or maybe he’s doing too much of a twist, either way, it always hits the ‘meh’ for me <br><br>I don’t really have much to say beyond that <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512144050i/24577931._SY540_.png" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i> “It's turtles all the way down,” she laughs. “It's turtles all the way fucking down,” Daisy agrees </i><br><br>3.5 stars!!<br><br><br>3.5 stars!!<br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br>i'm honestly not john green's //biggest fan// but hey how can you NOT read a john green book amirite?<br><br>i just dont want any 16 year old philosophers :|</span>
  <a data-text-id="4221305891680089783" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_18460392'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18460392-all-the-bright-places"><img alt="All the Bright Places" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1404331702l/18460392._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1GOVpA9MxRTpCCzLLTXcSxlsGRzJEYOsxOGu4n/Dt7PuRfx2tBIMfE4jmKrawNaUzzP+1AecDcufn+hTsoBFKQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+AaeeRZiDhTaMlRKC0+bvlBIZ1tv42fpDgVaMwHL2iXCIPerrTzHfH0Z4Cv8upFhhheAk6Fu6Y5VexyCzIgovw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/1406384.John_Green">About John Green</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/1406384.John_Green"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1353452301p3/1406384.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/1406384.John_Green">John Green
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
275,351
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer446759846851790091"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br/><br/>John Green's first novel, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/99561.Looking_for_Alaska' title='Looking for Alaska by John Green' rel='nofollow noopener'>Looking for Alaska</a>, won the 2006 Michael L. Printz Award presented by the American Library Association. His second novel, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/49750.An_Abundance_of_Katherines' title='An Abundance of Katherines by John Green' rel='nofollow noopener'>An Abundance of Katherines</a>, was a 2007 Michael L. Printz Award Honor Book and a finalist for the Los Angeles Times Book Prize. His next novel, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2914097.Paper_Towns' title='Paper Towns by John Green' rel='nofollow noopener'>Paper Towns</a>, is a New </span>
  <span id="freeText446759846851790091" style="display:none"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br /><br />John Green's first novel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/99561.Looking_for_Alaska" title="Looking for Alaska by John Green" rel="nofollow noopener">Looking for Alaska</a>, won the 2006 Michael L. Printz Award presented by the American Library Association. His second novel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/49750.An_Abundance_of_Katherines" title="An Abundance of Katherines by John Green" rel="nofollow noopener">An Abundance of Katherines</a>, was a 2007 Michael L. Printz Award Honor Book and a finalist for the Los Angeles Times Book Prize. His next novel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2914097.Paper_Towns" title="Paper Towns by John Green" rel="nofollow noopener">Paper Towns</a>, is a New York Times bestseller and won the Edgar Allen Poe Award for Best YA Mystery. In January 2012, his most recent novel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11870085.The_Fault_in_Our_Stars" title="The Fault in Our Stars by John Green" rel="nofollow noopener">The Fault in Our Stars</a>, was met with wide critical acclaim, unprecedented in Green's career. The praise included rave reviews in Time Magazine and The New York Times, on NPR, and from award-winning author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/11466.Markus_Zusak" title="Markus Zusak" rel="nofollow noopener">Markus Zusak</a>. The book also topped the New York Times Children's Paperback Bestseller list for several weeks. Green has also coauthored a book with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/11664.David_Levithan" title="David Levithan" rel="nofollow noopener">David Levithan</a> called <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6567017.Will_Grayson__Will_Grayson" title="Will Grayson, Will Grayson by John Green" rel="nofollow noopener">Will Grayson, Will Grayson</a>, published in 2010. The film rights for all his books, with the exception of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6567017.Will_Grayson__Will_Grayson" title="Will Grayson, Will Grayson by John Green" rel="nofollow noopener">Will Grayson Will Grayson</a>, have been optioned to major Hollywood Studios.<br /><br />In 2007, John and his brother Hank were the hosts of a popular internet blog, "<a href="http://www.brotherhood2.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Brotherhood 2.0</a>," where they discussed their lives, books and current events every day for a year except for weekends and holidays. They still keep a video blog, now called "The Vlog Brothers," which can be found on the <a href="http://nerdfighters.ning.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Nerdfighters</a> website, or a direct link <a href="http://youtube.com/vlogbrothers" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="446759846851790091" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
